And not Lamb Pie! Same goes with Takoyaki. When I want Takoyaki, I want the real one, with Tako as the filling. That is why it is called TAKOYAKI!I want real Takoyaki! Not a fake one! Sure it does looks like Takoyaki but is it really Takoyaki?! I doubt that! How do you feel when people told you that what you eat is Chicken Pie, when in fact it is Lamb Pie! That is just straight up deceiving!And this is one of my pet peeves whenever seller claiming that the Takoyaki is Takoyaki, when truthfully it is not even Takoyaki! There goes my trust issue.It would no longer be called 'Takoyaki' anymore if the filling is, for example a shrimp. It would be called 'Ebiyaki'. Takoyaki is Octopus Ball. O C T O P U S BALL! O . C . T . O . P . U . S !I do not trust those sellers who sells so called 'Takoyaki' when in fact, it is not even 'Takoyaki', but other than the tako itself! ğŸ™„ FACT! - TAKO is an Octopus!
